REMARKS.The_NNP repor_NN s_NN now_RB under_IN review_NN cover_VBP the_DT plague_JJ history_NN of_IN the_DT Punjab_NNP during_IN the_DT two_CD years_NNS 1901-02_JJ and_CC 1902-03_JJ ,_, and_CC in_IN addition_NN give_VBP the_DT history_NN of_IN anti-plague_JJ inoculations_NNS in_IN the_DT Province_NNP during_IN 1900-01_JJ ,_, During_IN the_DT two_CD latter_JJR years_NNS the_DT people_NNS had_VBD nothing_NN to_TO fear_VB from_IN reporting_VBG plague_NN as_IN no_DT compulsory_NN measures_NNS were_VBD in_IN force_NN ,_, and_CC it_PRP is_VBZ believed_VBN that_IN reports_NNS of_IN cases_NNS and_CC deaths_NNS were_VBD freely_RB made_VBN ._.

An_DT instance_NN of_IN the_DT breakdown_NN of_IN reporting_NN is_VBZ afforded_VBN by_IN Gujrnwla_NNP ,_, in_IN which_WDT district_NN deaths_NNS only_RB appear_VBP to_TO have_VB been_VBN brought_VBN on_IN to_TO the_DT record_NN in_IN July_NNP 1903_CD :_: the_DT district_NN figures_NNS for_IN the_DT month_NN give_VBP 1,892_CD cases_NNS and_CC the_DT same_JJ number_NN of_IN deaths_NNS ._.
Moreover_RB ,_, the_DT monthly_JJ or_CC weekly_JJ returns_NNS were_VBD commonly_RB affected_VBN by_IN the_DT omission_NN to_TO report_VB cases_NNS and_CC deaths_NNS in_IN the_DT period_NN in_IN which_WDT they_PRP occurred_VBD and_CC their_PRP$ subsequent_JJ inclusion_NN in_IN a_DT later_JJ period_NN when_WRB they_PRP came_VBD to_TO light_NN ._.
The_DT inclusion_NN of_IN deaths_NNS which_WDT occurred_VBD previously_RB account_NN for_IN such_JJ returns_NNS as_IN that_DT of_IN Silkot_NNP during_IN June_NNP 1902_CD ,_, when_WRB 988_CD cases_NNS with_IN 1,010_CD deaths_NNS were_VBD reported_VBN ,_, or_CC that_IN of_IN Lahore_NNP for_IN June_NNP 1903_CD ,_, when_WRB 2,425_CD cases_NNS and_CC 6,867_CD deaths_NNS were_VBD reported_VBN ._.

1_CD ._.

?_. PART_NN I_PRP ._.

In_IN Table_NNP No_NNP ._.

2_CD 5_CD ._.
Statement_JJ No_NNP ._.

CHAPTER_NN V._NNP THE_NNP ``_`` PRECHING_NNP ''_'' OF_IN INOCULATIONS_NNP ._.
Points_NNS of_IN practical_JJ importance_NN for_IN every_DT one_CD to_TO consider_VB in_IN connexion_NN with_IN inoculation_NN in_IN plague-_JJ infected_JJ or_CC threatened_JJ places_NNS ._.
